   256	        memtest_fill_value(m, bytes, ULONG_ONEZERO, ULONG_ZEROONE, 'C', interactive);
   257	        if (interactive) memtest_progress_end();
   258	        errors += memtest_compare_times(m, bytes, pass, 4, interactive);
   259	    }
   260	    return errors;
   261	}
   262	
   263	/* A version of memtest_test() that tests memory in small pieces
   264	 * in order to restore the memory content at exit.
   265	 *
   266	 * One problem we have with this approach, is that the cache can avoid
   267	 * real memory accesses, and we can't test big chunks of memory at the
   268	 * same time, because we need to backup them on the stack (the allocator
   269	 * may not be usable or we may be already in an out of memory condition).
   270	 * So what we do is to try to trash the cache with useless memory accesses
   271	 * between the fill and compare cycles. */
   272	#define MEMTEST_BACKUP_WORDS (1024 * (1024 / sizeof(long)))
   273	/* Random accesses of MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE are performed at the start and
   274	 * end of the region between fill and compare cycles in order to trash
   275	 * the cache. */
   276	#define MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE (1024 * 8)
   277	
   278	NO_SANITIZE("undefined")
   279	int memtest_preserving_test(unsigned long *m, size_t bytes, int passes) {
   280	    unsigned long backup[MEMTEST_BACKUP_WORDS];
   281	    unsigned long *p = m;
   282	    unsigned long *end = (unsigned long *)(((unsigned char *)m) + (bytes - MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE));
   283	    size_t left = bytes;
   284	    int errors = 0;
   285	
   286	    if (bytes & 4095) return 0;     /* Can't test across 4k page boundaries. */
   287	    if (bytes < 4096 * 2) return 0; /* Can't test a single page. */
   288	
   289	    while (left) {
   290	        /* If we have to test a single final page, go back a single page
   291	         * so that we can test two pages, since the code can't test a single
   292	         * page but at least two. */
   293	        if (left == 4096) {
   294	            left += 4096;
   295	            p -= 4096 / sizeof(unsigned long);
   296	        }
   297	
   298	        int pass = 0;
   299	        size_t len = (left > sizeof(backup)) ? sizeof(backup) : left;
   300	
   301	        /* Always test an even number of pages. */
   302	        if (len / 4096 % 2) len -= 4096;
   303	
   304	        memcpy(backup, p, len); /* Backup. */
   305	        while (pass != passes) {
   306	            pass++;
   307	            errors += memtest_addressing(p, len, 0);
   308	            memtest_fill_random(p, len, 0);
   309	            if (bytes >= MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE) {
   310	                memtest_compare_times(m, MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE, pass, 1, 0);
   311	                memtest_compare_times(end, MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE, pass, 1, 0);
   312	            }
   313	            errors += memtest_compare_times(p, len, pass, 4, 0);
   314	            memtest_fill_value(p, len, 0, (unsigned long)-1, 'S', 0);
   315	            if (bytes >= MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE) {
   316	                memtest_compare_times(m, MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE, pass, 1, 0);
   317	                memtest_compare_times(end, MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE, pass, 1, 0);
   318	            }
   319	            errors += memtest_compare_times(p, len, pass, 4, 0);
   320	            memtest_fill_value(p, len, ULONG_ONEZERO, ULONG_ZEROONE, 'C', 0);
   321	            if (bytes >= MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE) {
   322	                memtest_compare_times(m, MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE, pass, 1, 0);
   323	                memtest_compare_times(end, MEMTEST_DECACHE_SIZE, pass, 1, 0);
   324	            }
   325	            errors += memtest_compare_times(p, len, pass, 4, 0);
   326	        }
   327	        memcpy(p, backup, len); /* Restore. */
   328	        left -= len;
   329	        p += len / sizeof(unsigned long);
   330	    }

  1957	#define MEMTEST_MAX_REGIONS 128
  1958	
  1959	/* A non destructive memory test executed during segfault. */
  1960	int memtest_test_linux_anonymous_maps(void) {
  1961	    FILE *fp;
  1962	    char line[1024];
  1963	    char logbuf[1024];
  1964	    size_t start_addr, end_addr, size;
  1965	    size_t start_vect[MEMTEST_MAX_REGIONS];
  1966	    size_t size_vect[MEMTEST_MAX_REGIONS];
  1967	    int regions = 0, j;
  1968	
  1969	    int fd = openDirectLogFiledes();
  1970	    if (fd == -1) return 0;
  1971	
  1972	    fp = fopen("/proc/self/maps", "r");
  1973	    if (!fp) {
  1974	        closeDirectLogFiledes(fd);
  1975	        return 0;
  1976	    }
  1977	    while (fgets(line, sizeof(line), fp) != NULL) {
  1978	        char *start, *end, *p = line;
  1979	
  1980	        start = p;
  1981	        p = strchr(p, '-');
  1982	        if (!p) continue;
  1983	        *p++ = '\0';
  1984	        end = p;
  1985	        p = strchr(p, ' ');
  1986	        if (!p) continue;
  1987	        *p++ = '\0';
  1988	        if (strstr(p, "stack") || strstr(p, "vdso") || strstr(p, "vsyscall")) continue;
  1989	        if (!strstr(p, "00:00")) continue;
  1990	        if (!strstr(p, "rw")) continue;
  1991	
  1992	        start_addr = strtoul(start, NULL, 16);
  1993	        end_addr = strtoul(end, NULL, 16);
  1994	        size = end_addr - start_addr;
  1995	
  1996	        start_vect[regions] = start_addr;
  1997	        size_vect[regions] = size;
  1998	        snprintf(logbuf, sizeof(logbuf), "*** Preparing to test memory region %lx (%lu bytes)\n",
  1999	                 (unsigned long)start_vect[regions], (unsigned long)size_vect[regions]);
  2000	        if (write(fd, logbuf, strlen(logbuf)) == -1) { /* Nothing to do. */
  2001	        }
  2002	        regions++;
  2003	    }
  2004	
  2005	    int errors = 0;
  2006	    for (j = 0; j < regions; j++) {
  2007	        if (write(fd, ".", 1) == -1) { /* Nothing to do. */
  2008	        }
  2009	        errors += memtest_preserving_test((void *)start_vect[j], size_vect[j], 1);
  2010	        if (write(fd, errors ? "E" : "O", 1) == -1) { /* Nothing to do. */
  2011	        }
  2012	    }
  2013	    if (write(fd, "\n", 1) == -1) { /* Nothing to do. */
  2014	    }
  2015	
  2016	    /* NOTE: It is very important to close the file descriptor only now
  2017	     * because closing it before may result into unmapping of some memory
  2018	     * region that we are testing. */
  2019	    fclose(fp);
  2020	    closeDirectLogFiledes(fd);
  2021	    return errors;
  2022	}

  2025	static void killMainThread(void) {
  2026	    int err;
  2027	    if (pthread_self() != server.main_thread_id && pthread_cancel(server.main_thread_id) == 0) {
  2028	        if ((err = pthread_join(server.main_thread_id, NULL)) != 0) {
  2029	            serverLog(LL_WARNING, "main thread can not be joined: %s", strerror(err));
  2030	        } else {
  2031	            serverLog(LL_WARNING, "main thread terminated");
  2032	        }
  2033	    }
  2034	}
  2035	
  2036	/* Kill the running threads (other than current) in an unclean way. This function
  2037	 * should be used only when it's critical to stop the threads for some reason.
  2038	 * Currently the server does this only on crash (for instance on SIGSEGV) in order
  2039	 * to perform a fast memory check without other threads messing with memory. */
  2040	void killThreads(void) {
  2041	    killMainThread();
  2042	    bioKillThreads();
  2043	    killIOThreads();
  2044	}

  3690	                    clusterDelNode(link->node);
  3691	                    return 0;

    76	    printf("\x1b[H\x1b[2J"); /* Cursor home, clear screen. */

    81	    printf("\x1b[H\x1b[2K");          /* Cursor home, clear current line.  */

    83	    progress_printed = 0;

cat > /tmp/repro_asan_memtest.sh <<'EOF'
#!/bin/sh
set -eu
cat > /tmp/repro_asan_memtest.c <<'C'
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <unistd.h>

int main(void) {
    FILE *fp = fopen("/proc/self/maps", "r");
    char line[1024];
    if (!fp) return 2;
    while (fgets(line, sizeof(line), fp)) {
        char orig[1024];
        char *start, *end, *p;
        unsigned long s, e, len;
        memcpy(orig, line, sizeof(orig));
        p = line;
        start = p;
        p = strchr(p, '-');
        if (!p) continue;
        *p++ = '\0';
        end = p;
        p = strchr(p, ' ');
        if (!p) continue;
        *p++ = '\0';
        if (strstr(p, "stack") || strstr(p, "vdso") || strstr(p, "vsyscall")) continue;
        if (!strstr(p, "00:00")) continue;
        if (!strstr(p, "rw")) continue;
        s = strtoul(start, NULL, 16);
        e = strtoul(end, NULL, 16);
        len = e - s;
        if (len < 8192) continue;
        if (len > 1024*1024) len = 1024*1024;
        fprintf(stderr, "copying %lu bytes from %lx (%s)", len, s, orig);
        char *backup = malloc(len);
        if (!backup) return 3;
        memcpy(backup, (void *)s, len);
        free(backup);
    }
    fclose(fp);
    return 0;
}
C

The root cause appears to be the crash-time fast memory test scanning anonymous read/write mappings from `/proc/self/maps`. Under AddressSanitizer, those mappings include ASan shadow memory. The preserving memory test then copies and overwrites those pages, corrupting ASan’s metadata and producing the secondary sanitizer crash seen in the PR. The minimal safe behavior is to not run Valkey’s crash memory test when the binary itself is built with AddressSanitizer.

🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_asan.sh <<'EOF'
#!/bin/sh
set -eu
cd /testbed
cat > /tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_asan.c <<'C'
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <unistd.h>

int memtest_preserving_test(unsigned long *m, size_t bytes, int passes);

int main(void) {
    FILE *fp = fopen("/proc/self/maps", "r");
    char line[1024];
    if (!fp) return 2;
    while (fgets(line, sizeof(line), fp)) {
        char *start, *end, *p = line;
        unsigned long start_addr, end_addr, size;
        start = p;
        p = strchr(p, '-');
        if (!p) continue;
        *p++ = '\0';
        end = p;
        p = strchr(p, ' ');
        if (!p) continue;
        *p++ = '\0';
        if (strstr(p, "stack") || strstr(p, "vdso") || strstr(p, "vsyscall")) continue;
        if (!strstr(p, "00:00")) continue;
        if (!strstr(p, "rw")) continue;
        start_addr = strtoul(start, NULL, 16);
        end_addr = strtoul(end, NULL, 16);
        size = end_addr - start_addr;
        if (size < 8192) continue;
        fprintf(stderr, "testing %lx-%lx (%lu bytes)\n", start_addr, end_addr, size);
        memtest_preserving_test((void *)start_addr, size, 1);
    }
    fclose(fp);
    return 0;
}
C
cc -fsanitize=address -g -O1 -fno-omit-frame-pointer -I src /tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_asan.c src/memtest.c -o /tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_asan
/tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_asan
EOF

cat > /tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_guarded_asan.sh <<'EOF'
#!/bin/sh
set -eu
cd /testbed
cat > /tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_guarded_asan.c <<'C'
#include "config.h"
#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <unistd.h>

int memtest_preserving_test(unsigned long *m, size_t bytes, int passes);
void _serverAssert(const char *estr, const char *file, int line) {
    fprintf(stderr, "assertion failed: %s at %s:%d\n", estr, file, line);
    abort();
}

int main(void) {
#if defined(HAVE_PROC_MAPS) && !defined(VALKEY_ADDRESS_SANITIZER)
    FILE *fp = fopen("/proc/self/maps", "r");
    char line[1024];
    if (!fp) return 2;
    while (fgets(line, sizeof(line), fp)) {
        char *start, *end, *p = line;
        unsigned long start_addr, end_addr, size;
        start = p;
        p = strchr(p, '-');
        if (!p) continue;
        *p++ = '\0';
        end = p;
        p = strchr(p, ' ');
        if (!p) continue;
        *p++ = '\0';
        if (strstr(p, "stack") || strstr(p, "vdso") || strstr(p, "vsyscall")) continue;
        if (!strstr(p, "00:00")) continue;
        if (!strstr(p, "rw")) continue;
        start_addr = strtoul(start, NULL, 16);
        end_addr = strtoul(end, NULL, 16);
        size = end_addr - start_addr;
        if (size < 8192) continue;
        fprintf(stderr, "testing %lx-%lx (%lu bytes)\n", start_addr, end_addr, size);
        memtest_preserving_test((void *)start_addr, size, 1);
    }
    fclose(fp);
#else
    fprintf(stderr, "fast memory test skipped for AddressSanitizer build\n");
#endif
    return 0;
}
C

/tmp/repro_valkey_memtest_guarded_asan
